  • MINISTERIAL DELEGATIONS TO WASHINGTON INTERNATIONAL RENEWABLE ENERGY CONFERENCE REF: A) STATE 138248, B) GODFREY-LAWSON E-MAIL 11/21/2007 Per reftel, Post requests that Libya be added to the list of invitees for the March 2008 Washington International Renewable Energy Conference (WIREC). The GOL has demonstrated keen interest in developing its renewable energy sector and could represent a sizeable market for renewable technologies in the future. In addition, scientific engagement and cooperation have constituted an important component of the re-establishment of formal U.S.-Libyan diplomatic ties; participation by the GOL in the WIREC 2008 event would represent another significant step in the re-establishment of regular government-to-government ties outside the strictly political sphere. MILAM 0 11/26/2007

  • DEMARCHE GIVEN: U.S.-CANADA-MEXICO TRILATERAL PROPOSAL TO ADD HYDROFLUOROCARBONS TO THE MONTREAL PROTOCOL REF: STATE 95899 (U) On September 24, Econoff delivered ref demarche to MFA Environment and Sustainable Development Department Counselor Amr Abdel-Wareth regarding the U.S-Canada-Mexico trilateral proposal to add hydrofluorocarbons to the Montreal Protocol on Substances that deplete the Ozone Layer. Abdel-Wareth, who started his position less than a month ago, said he would review the proposal and share it with his colleagues. He indicated that planning is under way for the November Montreal Protocol meeting in Port Ghalib, Egypt and that the Prime Minister and Minister of Environment are scheduled to attend. Post will report any substantive Egyptian response septel. Scobey

  • AARGH! SWEDISH PIRATES SET SAIL FOR BRUSSELS 1. Summary and Comment: Swedens two largest political parties, the ruling Moderates and opposition Social Democrats, saw little change over their 2004 levels of support in the June 7 European Parliament (EP) election here. Instead, the Greens and the pro-EU Liberal Party were the big winners -- along with the new Pirate Party, which found support from young voters unhappy with the governments decision to shut down The Pirate Bay, a file-sharing bit torrent site that had become a target of the Motion Picture Association of America (and USTR). The anti-EU Left Party, on the other hand, suffered catastrophic losses. Overall, voter turnout was up in the month before Sweden takes over the rotating Presidency of the Council of the European Union, but at 43.8% still far below the regular 80% turnout for national elections. Comment: The EP election outcome has little predictive power for next years parliamentary elections, given the self-selecting nature of those willing to go out and vote for Members of the European Parliament (MEPs). Perhaps the main lesson for the larger parties relates to the need to court the youth vote in more effective ways. End Summary and Comment.

    09STOCKHOLM355
